WordPress.org is the home of the free, open-source WordPress software that you can install on your own web host. It offers full customization but requires more hands-on management. On the other hand, WordPress.com is a hosting service that offers a simplified version of WordPress, with hosting included. It's easier to use but comes with limitations in terms of monetization and customization.
